<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 27pt"><i>&#160;</i></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 27pt"><i>Appointment of Chief Financial Officer</i></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 27pt">On January 4, 2025, the Board of Directors (the
&#8220;Board&#8221;) of Lantronix, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) appointed Brent Stringham as the Company&#8217;s Chief Financial Officer
effective as of January 6, 2025.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 27pt">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 27pt">Mr. Stringham, age 46, has been serving as the Company&#8217;s
Chief Accounting Officer and Interim Chief Financial Officer since September 2024. Previously, Mr. Stringham served as the Company&#8217;s
Senior Director of Finance and Corporate Controller since February 2012.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 27pt">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 27pt">There are no arrangements or understandings between
Mr. Stringham and any other persons pursuant to which he was selected as an officer of the Company. There are also no family relationships
between Mr. Stringham and any director or executive officer of the Company, and Mr. Stringham does not have any direct or indirect material
interest in any transaction required to be disclosed pursuant to Item 404(a) of Regulation S-K.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 27pt">In connection with Mr. Stringham&#8217;s appointment
as Chief Financial Officer, the Company entered into an Amendment to Mr. Stringham&#8217;s employment agreement with the Company dated
January 6, 2025 (the &#8220;Amendment&#8221;), which includes the following compensation for Mr. Stringham:</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 27pt"/><td style="width: 18pt">&#8226;</td><td>Mr. Stringham will be entitled to an annual base salary of $310,000.</td></tr>
<tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td>&#160;</td><td>&#160;</td><td>&#160;</td></tr>
<tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 27pt"/><td style="width: 18pt">&#8226;</td><td>Mr. Stringham will be entitled to an annual incentive bonus opportunity based on the achievement of performance criteria to be established
by the Board (or a committee thereof). Mr. Stringham&#8217;s annual target bonus opportunity will be 50% of his base salary for the corresponding
fiscal year (effective as of January 1, 2025).</td></tr></table>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 27pt">The foregoing description of the Amendment is a
summary, does not purport to be complete and is qualified in its entirety by reference to the Amendment, which is attached hereto as Exhibit
10.1 and is incorporated herein by reference.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><b>&#160;</b></p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0"/><td style="width: 1in"><b>Item 7.01</b></td><td><b>Regulation FD Disclosure.</b></td></tr></table>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 27pt; background-color: white">On January 10, 2025, the
Company issued a press release announcing the appointment&#160;of Mr. Stringham as Chief Financial Officer&#160;effective on January 6,
2025. A copy of the press release is furnished as Exhibit 99.1 to this Current Report on Form 8-K and incorporated by reference.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 27pt; background-color: white">The information contained
in Item 7.01 of this Current Report on Form 8-K (including Exhibit 99.1 hereto) shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for the purposes
of Section 18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities
of that section, nor shall it be, or be deemed, incorporated by reference in any filings under the&#160;Securities Act of 1933, as amended
(the &#8220;Securities Act&#8221;), unless the Company specifically states that the information is to be considered &#8220;filed&#8221;
under the&#160;Exchange Act&#160;or incorporates it by reference into a filing under the&#160;Securities Act&#160;or the&#160;Exchange
Act.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&#160;</p>

<DESCRIPTION>AMENDMENT TO LETTER AGREEMENT, DATED AS OF JANUARY 6, 2025, BETWEEN BRENT STRINGHAM AND LANTRONIX, INC.
<TEXT>

<HEAD>
     <TITLE></TITLE>
</HEAD>
<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="margin: 0"><B>Exhibit 10.1</B></P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><IMG SRC="image_001.jpg" ALT="" STYLE="height: 38px; width: 238px"></P>
<P STYLE="margin: 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0"><B></B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">January 6, 2025</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><BR>
<BR>
</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Brent Stringham</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">c/o Lantronix, Inc.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">48 Discovery, Suite 250</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Irvine, CA 92618</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Dear Brent:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">We want to thank you for your dedicated service
to Lantronix, Inc (&ldquo;Lantronix&rdquo; or &ldquo;Company&rdquo;) since 2012 and to confirm the terms of your promotion as set forth
in this letter. Your position and title with the Company will be Chief Financial Officer effective January 6, 2025, subject to the terms
and conditions of the certain letter agreement, dated as of September 13, 2024, by and between you and the Company (the &ldquo;Letter
Agreement&rdquo;), as amended herein.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">In the Letter Agreement, the section titled &ldquo;<B>BASE
SALARY&rdquo;</B> is hereby amended to read as follows:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.5in; text-align: justify">&ldquo;While you are employed with the
Company as Chief Financial Officer, the Company shall pay you a bi-weekly base salary in the amount of <B>$11,923.08 ($310,000.00 on an
annualized basis)</B>, less applicable withholdings and deductions, paid on the Company&rsquo;s regular bi-weekly payroll dates. You will
be classified as an exempt employee, and your salary will be paid on a salary basis and is intended to compensate you for all hours that
you work. Your salary will be reviewed at the time executive salaries are reviewed periodically, and the Company may, in its sole discretion,
adjust it to reflect Company performance, your performance, market conditions, and other factors deemed relevant by the Company.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">In the Letter Agreement, the section titled &ldquo;<B>BONUS&rdquo;</B>
is hereby amended to read as follows:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.5in; text-align: justify">&ldquo;While you are employed with the
Company as Chief Financial Officer, you will be eligible to participate in Lantronix&rsquo;s Annual Bonus Program (&ldquo;Program&rdquo;)
at a target amount that will be equal to <B>50%</B> of your base salary. Your bonus percentage is not guaranteed and may be adjusted upward
or downward by the Compensation Committee of the Company&rsquo;s Board of Directors (the &ldquo;Compensation Committee&rdquo;) in its
sole discretion. Your participation will commence with the Fiscal 2025 plan period, which began July 1, 2024 and ends June 30, 2025. For
the purpose of calculating the bonus for the Fiscal 2025 plan period, the &ldquo;Base Salary&rdquo; used shall be the actual base salary
received by you during the applicable bonus period calculated as follows: (i) a target amount equal to 40% of the Base Salary received
from July 1, 2024 through December 31, 2024, and (ii) a target amount equal to 50% of your Base Salary received from January 1, 2025 through
June 30, 2025. Your participation and payment of a bonus and the amount is subject to the terms of the Program and the performance targets
established thereunder by the Compensation Committee, as such Programs and targets may be amended from time to time and are generally
established every year by the Compensation Committee. Lantronix reserves the right to change or discontinue the Program at any time, and
any right to a bonus is subject to your continued employment with the Company through the date that such bonus is actually paid to you.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"></P>

<DESCRIPTION>PRESS PRESS RELEASE OF LANTRONIX, INC. ISSUED ON JANUARY 10, 2025
<TEXT>
<HTML>
<HEAD>
     <TITLE></TITLE>
</HEAD>
<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="margin: 0"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><IMG SRC="image_002.jpg" ALT="logo.jpg" STYLE="height: 43px; width: 238px"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 18pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><B>Lantronix Names Brent Stringham as CFO </B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><I>&nbsp;</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>IRVINE, Calif.,</B> <FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">Jan. 10, 2025</FONT>
&mdash; Lantronix Inc.
(NASDAQ: LTRX) (the &ldquo;Company&rdquo;), a global leader in IoT compute and connectivity IoT solutions, today announced the appointment
of Brent Stringham as its chief financial officer (CFO). Stringham has been an experienced financial leader with Lantronix since 2012
and previously served as the Company&rsquo;s interim CFO and Chief Accounting Officer.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&ldquo;Brent brings deep institutional knowledge and extensive financial
expertise to his new role as CFO based on his many contributions to Lantronix over the past 13 years<FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">,&rdquo;
said Saleel Awsare</FONT>, chief executive officer of Lantronix. &ldquo;With Brent&rsquo;s financial leadership, Lantronix remains firmly
committed to delivering shareholder value and advancing its strategic objective focused on Edge Intelligence in the IoT industry.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Prior to joining Lantronix, Stringham held financial positions with
<FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">Iteris Inc., Netlist Inc. </FONT>and <FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">Ernst &amp; Young. Stringham
holds a bachelor&rsquo;s degree in Business Administration and Accounting from California State University in Fullerton, Calif., and is
a licensed Certified Public Accountant. </FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>About Lantronix</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Lantronix Inc. is a global leader of compute and connectivity IoT solutions
that target high-growth industries including Smart Cities, Automotive and Enterprise. Lantronix&rsquo;s products and services empower
companies to succeed in the growing IoT markets by delivering customizable solutions that address each layer of the IoT Stack. Lantronix&rsquo;s
leading-edge solutions include Intelligent Substations infrastructure, Infotainment systems and Video Surveillance, supplemented with
advanced Out-of-Band Management (OOBM) for Cloud and Edge Computing.&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">For more information, visit the Lantronix
website.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><I>&ldquo;Safe Harbor&rdquo; Statement under the Private Securities
Litigation Reform Act of 1995:&nbsp;This news release contains forward-looking statements within the meaning of federal securities laws,
including, without limitation, statements related to Lantronix leadership.&nbsp;These forward-looking statements are based on our current
expectations and are subject to&nbsp;substantial&nbsp;risks and uncertainties that could cause&nbsp;our actual results, future business,

the restrictions in our debt agreements; and any additional factors included in our Annual Report on Form 10-K for the fiscal year ended
June 30, 2024, filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission (the &ldquo;SEC&rdquo;) on Sept. 9, 2024, including in the section entitled
